The original format\n// used string references that could break when datasources were renamed, moved between organizations,\n// or when multiple datasources shared similar names. This created reliability and portability issues\n// for dashboard sharing and automation workflows.\n//\n// The migration works by:\n// 1. Processing annotations, template variables, and panels (including nested panels in rows)\n// 2. Converting string datasource references to structured objects containing uid, type, and apiVersion\n// 3. Handling null/missing datasource references by setting appropriate defaults\n// 4. Maintaining consistency between panel and target datasource configurations\n// 5. Preserving special datasource types like Mixed datasources and expression queries\n//\n// This transformation provides several critical benefits:\n// - Eliminates datasource reference breakage when datasources are renamed\n// - Enables reliable dashboard export/import across different Grafana instances\n// - Supports advanced datasource features that require type and version information\n// - Prepares the schema for future datasource management enhancements\n// - Maintains backward compatibility while establishing a robust foundation\n//\n// The migration handles complex scenarios including:\n// - Panels with missing datasource configuration (set to default)\n// - Mixed datasource panels with heterogeneous targets\n// - Expression queries that reference other queries\n// - Template variables that depend on datasource queries\n// - Annotation queries from various datasource types\n//\n// Example transformations:\n//\n// Before migration (string reference):\n//\n//\tdatasource: \"prometheus-prod\"\n//\t// or\n//\tdatasource: null\n//\n// After migration (structured object):\n//\n//\tdatasource: {\n//\t  uid: \"prometheus-uid-123\",\n//\t  type: \"prometheus\",\n//\t  apiVersion: \"v1\"\n//\t}\n//\n// Before migration (panel with targets):\n//\n//\tpanel: {\n//\t  datasource: \"CloudWatch\",\n//\t  targets: [{\n//\t    datasource: null,\n//\t    refId: \"A\"\n//\t  }]\n//\t}\n//\n// After migration (consistent references):\n//\n//\tpanel: {\n//\t  datasource: {\n//\t    uid: \"cloudwatch-uid-456\",\n//\t    type: 575→      this.migrateCloudWatchAnnotationQuery();\n   576→    }\n   577→\n   578→    if (oldVersion < 35 && finalTargetVersion >= 35) {\n   579→      panelUpgrades.push(ensureXAxisVisibility);\n   580→    }\n   581→\n   582→    if (oldVersion < 36 && finalTargetVersion >= 36) {\n   583→      // Migrate datasource to refs in annotations\n   584→      for (const query of this.dashboard.templating.list) {\n   592→          if (variable.type === 'query' && variable.datasource === null) {\n   593→            variable.datasource = getDataSourceRef(defaultDs);\n   594→          }\n   595→        }\n   596→\n   597→        panelUpgrades.push((panel: PanelModel) => {\n   598→          if (panel.targets) {\n   599→            let panelDataSourceWasDefault = false;\n   600→            if (panel.datasource == null && panel.targets.length > 0) {\n   601→              panel.datasource = getDataSourceRef(defaultDs);\n   602→              panelDataSourceWasDefault = true;\n   603→            }\n   604→\n   605→            for (const target of panel.targets) {\n   606→              if (target.datasource == null || target.datasource.uid == null) {\n   607→                if // In this case we use the query level data source as source for truth\n   617→                panel.datasource = target.datasource;\n   618→              }\n   619→            }\n   620→          }\n   621→          return panel;\n   622→        });\n   623→      }\n   624→    }\n   625→\n   626→    if (oldVersion < 37 && finalTargetVersion >= 37) {\n   627→      panelUpgrades.push((panel: PanelModel) => {\n   628→        if (panel.options?.legend && typeof panel.options.legend === 'object') {\n   629→          // There were two ways to hide the legend, this normalizes to `legend.showLegend`\n   630→          if (panel.options.legend.displayMode === 'hidden' || panel.options.legend.showLegend === false) {\n   631→            panel.options.legend.displayMode = 'list';\n 636→        }\n   637→\n   638→        return panel;\n   639→      });\n   640→    }\n   641→\n   642→    // Update old table cell display configuration to the new\n   643→    // format which uses an object for configuration\n   644→    if (oldVersion < 38 && finalTargetVersion >= 38) {\n   645→      panelUpgrades.push((panel: PanelModel) => {\n   646→        if (panel.type === 'table' && }\n   657→\n   658→          // Update any overrides referencing the cell display mode\n   659→          if (panel.fieldConfig?.overrides) {\n   660→            for (const override of 663→                if (override.properties[j].id === 'custom.displayMode') {\n   664→                  override.properties[j].id = 'custom.cellOptions';\n   665→                  override.properties[j].value = migrateTableDisplayModeToCellOptions(overrideDisplayMode);\n   666→                }\n   667→              }\n   668→            }\n   669→          }\n   670→        }\n   671→\n   672→        return panel;\n   673→      });\n   674→    }\n   675→\n   676→    // Update the configuration of the Timeseries to table transformation\n   677→    // to support multiple panel.transformations?.forEach((transformation) => {\n   681→          // If we run into a timeSeriesTable transformation\n   682→          // and it doesn't have undefined options then we migrate\n   683→          if (\n   684→            transformation.id === 'timeSeriesTable' &&\n   685→            transformation.options !== undefined &&\n   686→            transformation.options.refIdToStat !==   }\n   704→        });\n   705→\n   706→        return panel;\n   707→      });\n   708→    }\n   709→\n   710→    if (oldVersion < 40 && finalTargetVersion >= 40) {\n   711→      // In old 717→    if (oldVersion < 41 && finalTargetVersion >= 41) {\n   718→      // time_options is a legacy property that was not used since grafana version 5\n   719→      //  therefore deprecating this 742→        for (k = 0; k < panelUpgrades.length; k++) {\n   743→          this.dashboard.panels[j] = panelUpgrades[k].call(this, this.dashboard.panels[j]);\n   744→          const rowPanels = upgrades\n   755→    // Only update schema version if migrations were actually needed\n   756→    if (oldVersion < finalTargetVersion) {\n   757→      this.dashboard.schemaVersion = finalTargetVersion;\n   758→    }\n   759→  }\n   760→\n   761→  private removeRepeatedPanels() {\n   762→    const newPanels = [];\n   763→\n   764→    for (const panel of this.dashboard.panels) {\n   765→      // @ts-expect-error\n   766→      if (panel.repeatPanelId || panel.repeatByRow) {\n   767→        continue;\n   768→      }\n   769→\n   770→      // Filter out repeats in collapsed rows\n migration, are put at the end of the array.\n   784→  migrateCloudWatchQueries(panel: PanelModel) {\n   785→    for (const target of panel.targets || []) {\n   786→      if (isCloudWatchQuery(target)) panel.targets.push(newQuery);\n   793→          }\n   794→        }\n   795→      }\n   796→    }\n   797→  }\n   798→\n   799→  // Migrates CloudWatch annotation queries that use multiple statistics into separate queries.\n   800→  // For example, if an annotation query uses ['Max', 'Min'] statistics, it will be split into\n   801→  // two separate annotation queries - one with 'Max' and another with 'Min'.\n   802→  // The new annotation queries are added to the end of the annotations list.\n   803→  migrateCloudWatchAnnotationQuery() {\n   804→    for (const annotation of 807→        for (const newAnnotationQuery of newAnnotationQueries) {\n   808→          this.dashboard.annotations.list.push(newAnnotationQuery);\n   809→        }\n   810→      }\n   811→    }\n   812→  }\n   813→\n   814→  upgradeToGridLayout(old: any) {\n   815→    let yPos = 0;\n   816→    const widthFactor = GRID_COLUMN_COUNT / 12;\n   817→\n   818→    const maxPanelId =\n   819→      max(\n   820→        flattenDeep(\n   821→          map(old.rows, (row) => {\n   822→            return map(row.panels, 'id');\n   823→          })\n   824→        ).filter((id) => id != null)\n   825→      ) || 0;\n   826→    let nextRowId = maxPanelId + 1;\n   827→\n   828→    if (!old.rows) {\n   829→      return;\n   830→    }\n   831→\n   832→    // Add special \"row\" panels if even one row is collapsed, repeated or has visible title\n   833→    const showRows = some(old.rows, (row) => row.collapse || row.showTitle || row.repeat);\n   834→\n   835→    for (const row of old.rows) {\n   836→      if (row.repeatIteration) {\n   837→        continue;\n   838→      }\n   839→\n   840→      const height = row.height || DEFAULT_ROW_HEIGHT;\n   841→      const rowGridHeight = getGridHeight(height);\n   842→\n   843→      const rowPanel: any = {};\n   844→      let rowPanelModel: PanelModel | undefined;\n   845→\n   846→      if (showRows) {\n   847→        // add special row panel\n   848→        rowPanel.id = nextRowId;\n   849→        rowPanel.type = 'row';\n   850→        rowPanel.title = row.title;\n   851→        rowPanel.collapsed = row.collapse;\n   852→        rowPanel.repeat = row.repeat;\n   853→        rowPanel.panels = [];\n   854→        rowPanel.gridPos = {\n   855→          x: 0,\n   856→          y: yPos,\n   857→          w: GRID_COLUMN_COUNT,\n   858→          h: rowGridHeight,\n   859→        };\n   860→        rowPanelModel = new PanelModel(rowPanel);\n   861→        nextRowId++;\n   862→        yPos++;\n   863→      }\n   864→\n   865→      const rowArea = new RowArea(rowGridHeight, GRID_COLUMN_COUNT, yPos);\n   866→\n   867→      for (const panel of row.panels) {\n   868→        panel.span = panel.span || DEFAULT_PANEL_SPAN;\n   869→        if (panel.minSpan) {\n   870→          panel.minSpan = Math.min(GRID_COLUMN_COUNT, (GRID_COLUMN_COUNT / 12) * panel.minSpan);\n   871→        }\n   872→        const panelWidth = Math.floor(panel.span) * widthFactor;\n   873→        const panelHeight = panel.height ? getGridHeight(panel.height) : rowGridHeight;\n   874→\n   875→        const panelPos = rowArea.getPanelPosition(panelHeight, panelWidth);\n   876→        yPos = rowArea.yPos;\n   877→        panel.gridPos = {\n   878→          x: panelPos.x,\n   879→          y: yPos + panelPos.y,\n   880→          w: panelWidth,\n   881→          h: panelHeight,\n   882→        };\n   883→        rowArea.addPanel(panel.gridPos);\n   884→\n   885→        delete panel.span;\n   886→\n   887→      }\n   892→      }\n   893→\n   894→      if (rowPanelModel) {\n   895→        this.dashboard.panels.push(rowPanelModel);\n   896→      }\n   897→\n   898→      if (!(rowPanelModel && rowPanel.collapsed)) {\n   899→        yPos += rowGridHeight;\n   900→      }\n   901→    }\n   902→  }\n   903→}\n   904→\n   905→function getGridHeight(height: number | string) {\n   906→  if (isString(height)) {\n   907→    height = parseInt(height.replace('px', ''), 10);\n   908→  }\n   909→\n   910→  if (height < MIN_PANEL_HEIGHT) {\n   911→    height = MIN_PANEL_HEIGHT;\n   912→  }\n   913→\n   914→  const gridHeight = Math.ceil(height / (GRID_CELL_HEIGHT + GRID_CELL_VMARGIN));\n   915→  return gridHeight;\n   916→}\n   917→\n   918→/**\n   919→ * RowArea represents dashboard row filled by panels\n   920→ * area is an array of numbers represented filled column's cells like\n   921→ *  -----------------------\n   922→ * |******** ****\n   923→ * |******** ****\n   924→ * |********\n   925→ *  -----------------------\n   926→ *  33333333 2222 00000 ...\n   927→ */\n   928→class RowArea {\n   929→  area: number[];\n   930→  yPos: number;\n   931→  height: number;\n   932→\n   933→  constructor(height: number, width = GRID_COLUMN_COUNT, rowYPos = 0) {\n   934→    this.area = new Array(width).fill(0);\n   935→    this.yPos = rowYPos;\n   936→    this.height = height;\n   937→  }\n   938→\n   939→  reset() {\n   940→    this.area.fill(0);\n   941→  }\n   942→\n   943→  /**\n   944→   * Update area after adding the panel.\n   945→   */\n   946→  addPanel(gridPos: any) {\n   947→    for (let i = gridPos.x; i < gridPos.x + gridPos.w; i++) {\n   948→      if (!this.area[i] || gridPos.y + gridPos.h - this.yPos > this.area[i]) {\n   949→        this.area[i] = gridPos.y + gridPos.h - this.yPos;\n   950→      }\n   951→    }\n   952→    return this.area;\n   953→  }\n   954→\n   955→  /**\n   956→   * Calculate position for the new panel in the row.\n   957→   */\n   958→  getPanelPosition(panelHeight: number, panelWidth: number, callOnce = false): any {\n   959→    let startPlace, endPlace;\n   960→    let place;\n   961→    for (let i = this.area.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {\n   962→      if (this.height - this.area[i] > 0) {\n   963→        if (endPlace === undefined) {\n   964→          endPlace = i;\n   965→        } else {\n   966→          if (i < this.area.length - 1 && this.area[i] <= this.area[i + 1]) {\n   967→            startPlace = i;\n   968→          } else {\n   969→            break;\n   970→          }\n   971→        }\n   972→      } else {\n   973→        break;\n   974→      }\n   975→    }\n   976→\n   977→    if (startPlace !== undefined && endPlace !== undefined && endPlace - startPlace >= panelWidth - 1) {\n   978→      const yPos = max(this.area.slice(startPlace));\n   979→      place = {\n   980→        x: startPlace,\n   981→        y: yPos,\n   982→      };\n   983→    } else if (!callOnce) {\n   984→      // wrap to next row\n   985→      this.yPos += this.height;\n   986→      this.reset();\n   987→      return this.getPanelPosition(panelHeight, panelWidth, true);\n   988→    } else {\n   989→      return null;\n   990→    }\n   991→\n   992→    return place;\n   993→  }\n   994→}\n   995→\n   996→function upgradePanelLink(link: any): DataLink {\n   997→  let url = link.url;\n   998→\n   999→  if (!url && link.dashboard) {\n  1000→    url = `dashboard/db/${kbn.slugifyForUrl(link.dashboard)}`;\n  1001→  }\n  1002→\n  1003→  if (!url && link.dashUri) {\n  1004→    url = `dashboard/${link.dashUri}`;\n  1005→  }\n  1006→\n  1007→  // some models are incomplete and have no dashboard or dashUri\n  1008→  if (!url) {\n  1009→    url = '/';\n  1010→  }\n  1011→\n  1012→ urlUtil.appendQueryToUrl(url, `$${DataLinkBuiltInVars.includeVars}`);\n  1018→  }\n  1019→\n  1020→  if (link.params) {\n  1021→    url = urlUtil.appendQueryToUrl(url, link.params);\n  1022→  }\n  1023→\n  1024→  return {\n  1025→    url: url,\n  1026→    title: link.title,\n  1027→    targetBlank: link.targetBlank,\n  1028→  };\n  1029→}\n  1030→\n  1031→function updateVariablesSyntax(text: string) {\n  1032→  const legacyVariableNamesRegex = /(__series_name)|(\\$__series_name)|(__value_time)|(__field_name)|(\\$__field_name)/g;\n  1033→\n  1034→  return text.replace(legacyVariableNamesRegex, (match, seriesName, seriesName1, valueTime, fieldName, fieldName1) => {\n  1035→    if (seriesName) {\n  1036→      return '__series.name';\n  1037→    }\n  1038→    if (seriesName1) {\n  1039→      return '${__series.name}';\n  1040→    }\n  1041→    if (valueTime) {\n  1042→      return '__value.time';\n  1043→    }\n  1044→    if (fieldName) {\n  1045→      return '__field.name';\n  1046→    }\n  1047→    if (fieldName1) {\n  1048→      return '${__field.name}';\n  1049→    }\n  1050→    return match;\n  1051→  });\n  1052→}\n  1053→\n  1054→interface MigrateDatasourceNameOptions {\n  1055→  returnDefaultAsNull: boolean;\n  1056→}\n  1057→\n  1058→export function migrateDatasourceNameToRef(\n  1059→  nameOrRef: string | DataSourceRef | null | undefined,\n  1060→  options: MigrateDatasourceNameOptions\n  1061→): DataSourceRef | null {\n  1062→  if (options.returnDefaultAsNull && (nameOrRef == null || nameOrRef === 'default')) {\n  1063→    return null;\n  1064→  }\n  1065→\n  1066→  if (isDataSourceRef(nameOrRef)) {\n  1067→    return nameOrRef;\n  1068→  }\n  1069→\n  1070→  const ds = getDataSourceRef(ds);\n  1076→}\n  1077→\n  1078→// mutates transformations appending a new transformer after the existing one\n  1079→function appendTransformerAfter(panel: PanelModel, id: string, cfg: DataTransformerConfig) {\n  1080→  if (panel.transformations) {\n  1081→    const transformations: DataTransformerConfig[] = [];\n  1082→    for (const t of panel.transformations) {\n  1083→      transformations.push(t);\n  1084→      if (t.id === id) {\n  1085→        transformations.push({ ...cfg });\n  1086→      }\n  1087→    }\n  1088→    panel.transformations = transformations;\n  1089→  }\n  1090→  return panel;\n  1091→}\n  1092→\n  1093→function upgradeValueMappingsForPanel(panel: PanelModel) {\n  1094→  const fieldConfig = panel.fieldConfig;\n  1095→  if (!fieldConfig) {\n  1096→    return panel;\n  1097→  }\n  1098→\n  1099→  if (fieldConfig.defaults && fieldConfig.defaults.mappings) {\n  1100→    fieldConfig.defaults.mappings = upgradeValueMappings(\n  1101→      fieldConfig.defaults.mappings,\n  1102→      fieldConfig.defaults.thresholds\n  1103→    );\n  1104→  }\n  1105→\n  1106→  // Protect against no overrides\n  1107→  if (Array.isArray(fieldConfig.overrides)) {\n  1108→    for (const override of fieldConfig.overrides) {\n  1109→      for (const prop of override.properties) {\n  1110→        if (prop.id === 'mappings') {\n  1111→          prop.value = upgradeValueMappings(prop.value);\n  1112→        }\n  1113→      }\n  1114→    }\n  1115→  }\n  1116→\n  1117→  return panel;\n  1118→}\n  1119→\n  1120→function 1124→    target.hasOwnProperty('region') &&\n  1125→    target.hasOwnProperty('metricName')\n  1126→  );\n  1127→}\n  1128→\n  1129→function isLegacyCloudWatchAnnotationQuery(\n  1130→  target: );\n  1139→}\n  1140→\n  1141→function upgradeValueMappings(oldMappings: any, thresholds?: ThresholdsConfig): ValueMapping[] | undefined {\n  1142→  if (!oldMappings) {\n  1143→    return undefined;\n  1144→  }\n  1145→\n  1146→  const valueMaps: ValueMap = { type: MappingType.ValueToText, options: {} };\n  1147→  const newMappings: ValueMapping[] = [];\n  1148→\n  1149→  for (const old of oldMappings) {\n  1150→    // when migrating singlestat to stat/gauge, mappings are handled by panel type change handler used in that migration\n  1151→    if (old.type && old.options) {\n  1152→      // collect al value->text mappings in a single value map object. These are migrated by panel change handler as a separate value maps\n  1153→      if (old.type === MappingType.ValueToText) {\n  1154→        valueMaps.options = {\n  1155→          ...valueMaps.options,\n  1156→          ...old.options,\n  1157→        };\n  1158→      } else {\n  1159→        newMappings.push(old);\n  1160→      }\n  1161→      continue;\n  1162→    }\n  1163→\n  1164→    // Use the color we would have picked from thesholds\n  1165→    let color: string | undefined = undefined;\n  1166→    const numeric = parseFloat(old.text);\n  1167→    if map(old.rows, (row) => {\n            return map(row.panels, 'id');\n          })\n        ).filter((id) => id != null)\n      ) || 0;\n    let nextRowId = maxPanelId + 1;\n\n    if (!old.rows) {\n panels including nested ones\\n4. **Datasource resolution**: Backend uses DataSourceInfoProvider to resolve datasource UIDs\\n5. **Defaults application**: Frontend defaults applied before version `migrateAnnotations()`: Updates annotation datasources\\n  - `migrateTemplateVariables()`: Updates variable datasources\\n  - `migratePanels()`: Updates panel and target datasources\\n- **V37-V42.go**: Modern schema adjustments\\n\\n### Utility Functions\\n- **`datasource_utils.go`**: Datasource migration helpers\\n  - `MigrateDatasourceNameToRef()`: Converts string datasource names to structured references\\n  - `GetDataSourceRef()`: Creates datasource reference objects\\n  - `GetDefaultDSInstanceSettings()`: Retrieves default datasource\\n- **`migration_utils.go`**: Shared utility functions\\n  - `GetStringValue()`, `GetBoolValue()`, `GetIntValue()`, `GetFloatValue()`: Safe value extraction\\n  - `ConvertToFloat()`, `ConvertToInt()`: Type conversion\\n- **`frontend_defaults.go`**: Frontend defaults application\\n  - `applyFrontendDefaults()`: Applies DashboardModel constructor defaults\\n  - `applyPanelDefaults()`: Applies PanelModel constructor defaults\\n\\n## Frontend Migration System (TypeScript)\\n\\n### DashboardMigrator Class\\nLocated at `public/app/features/dashboard/state/DashboardMigrator.ts`, implements the frontend version migration logic:\\n- **`DASHBOARD_SCHEMA_VERSION` constant**: Currently set to 42 (FINAL version for v1 dashboard API)\\n- **`constructor(dashboardModel)`**: Initializes with DashboardModel instance\\n- **`updateSchema(old, targetSchemaVersion?)` method**: Main migration orchestration that:\\n  1. Updates schema version after all migrations\\n  5. Does NOT add new migrations after v42 (reserved for app platform)\\n\\n### Key Migration Implementations\\n- **Version 2**: Migrates services.filter structure\\n- **Version 6**: Converts pulldowns to annotations\\n- **Version 16**: Upgrades to grid layout from rows\\n- **Version 33**: Converts datasource names to UID-based references\\n- **Version 36**: Major datasource reference migration matching backend V36\\n  - Updates annotation datasources\\n  - Migrates template variable datasources\\n  - Handles null datasources by assigning defaults\\n  - Processes nested panels in collapsed rows\\n  - Migrates target datasources with panel-level inheritance\\n- **Version 37-42**: Legend, table display, and field config migrations\\n\\n### Helper Functions\\n- **`migrateDatasourceNameToRef()`**: Converts datasource references, handles null/default cases\\n- **`upgradeToGridLayout()`**: Converts legacy row-based layout to grid layout\\n- **CloudWatch-specific migrations**: Separate handlers for CloudWatch query and annotation migrations\\n\\n## Data Flow\\n\\nThe migration pipeline follows this sequence:\\n1. **Frontend requests migration**: DashboardMigrator.updateSchema() is called\\n2. **Backend migration**: Optional backend validation/migration via Migrate() function\\n3. **Panel upgrades**: Applied uniformly to all panels including nested ones\\n4. **Datasource resolution**: Backend uses DataSourceInfoProvider to resolve datasource UIDs\\n5. **Defaults application**: Frontend defaults applied before version migrations\\n6. **Version increment**: Schema version updated as migrations complete\\n\\n## Key Design Principles\\n\\n1. **Version 42 is final**: No new schema migrations allowed for v1 dashboard API (migration to app platform)\\n2. **Incremental migrations**: Each version handles one logical change\\n3. **Frontend-backend parity**: Backend V36 mirrors frontend V36 implementation\\n4. **Datasource abstraction**: DataSourceInfoProvider allows flexible datasource resolution\\n5. **Defaults-first approach**: Frontend defaults applied before version migrations to ensure consistency\\n6. **Panel ID uniqueness**: Enforced after all migrations to prevent conflicts\\n\\n## Repository\\n- **repo**: grafana/grafana\\n- **commit**: 26d36ec\\n\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

panels including nested ones\\n4. **Datasource resolution**: Backend uses DataSourceInfoProvider to resolve datasource UIDs\\n5. **Defaults application**: Frontend defaults applied before version migrations\\n6. **Version increment**: Schema version updated as migrations complete\\n\\n## Key Design Principles\\n\\n1. **Version 42 is final**: No new schema migrations allowed for v1 dashboard API (migration to app platform)\\n2. **Incremental migrations**: Each version handles one logical change\\n3. **Frontend-backend parity**: Backend V36 mirrors frontend V36 implementation\\n4.
